# <a name="archived-release-notes-for-monthly-channel"></a><span data-ttu-id="149cb-103">有关每月频道的已存档发行说明</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-103">Archived Release notes for Monthly Channel</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="149cb-104">我们为 Office 365 专业增强版、Visio Pro for Office 365、Project Online 桌面客户端和 Office 365 商业版提供了每月频道更新。这些发行说明提供了有关这些更新中所含新功能和非安全更新的信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-104">These release notes provide information about new features and non-security updates that are included in Monthly Channel updates to Office 365 ProPlus, Visio Pro for Office 365, Project Online Desktop Client and Office 365 Business.</span></span>

 > [!NOTE]
>- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-105">我们经常会过一段时间就将功能（有时甚至是修补程序）发布到每月频道更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-105">We often roll out features (and sometimes even fixes) to Monthly over a period of time.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="149cb-106">如果没有立即看到下述内容，则很快就会看到的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-106">If you don’t see something described below right away, you can expect it soon.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="149cb-107">了解更多</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-107">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/when-do-i-get-the-newest-features-in-for-office-365-da36192c-58b9-4bc9-8d51-bb6eed468516)
>- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-108">Office 365 专业增强版现有安装的 Microsoft Teams - 从 7 月初开始，Office 365 专业增强版（和 Office 365 商业版）的更新将包含 Microsoft Teams。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-108">Microsoft Teams on existing installations of Office 365 ProPlus - Beginning in early July, updates to Office 365 ProPlus (and Office 365 Business) will include Microsoft Teams.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="149cb-109">将添加 Teams 的日期取决于所使用的更新频道。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-109">The date when Teams will be added depends on which update channel you're using.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="149cb-110">有关详细信息, 请参阅[使用 Office 365 专业增强版部署 Microsoft Teams](/deployoffice/teams-install)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-110">Please refer to [Deploy Microsoft Teams with Office 365 ProPlus](/deployoffice/teams-install) for additional information.</span></span>


[//]: # (请勿移除错误详细信息内容结尾)

## <a name="version-2011-december-21"></a><span data-ttu-id="149cb-112">版本 2011：12 月 21 日</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-112">Version 2011: December 21</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="149cb-113">*版本 2011（内部版本 13426.20404）*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-113">*Version 2011 (Build 13426.20404)*</span></span>

### <a name="resolved-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="149cb-115">已解决的问题</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-115">Resolved issues</span></span>
### <a name="excel"></a><span data-ttu-id="149cb-116">Excel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-116">Excel</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-117">修复了以下问题：Excel 错误地显示新版本文件可用的消息栏，并强制用户将更改保存在工作簿副本中或放弃更改。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-117">Fixed an issue where Excel would incorrectly show a message bar that a new version of the file is available and force the user to save their changes in a copy of the workbook or discard their changes.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-118">修正了当打开包含 Excel 4.0 宏的 Excel 加载项文件时，Excel 可能会禁用宏而不提示的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-118">Fixed an issue where Excel may leave macros disabled without prompting when opening an Excel Add-in file containing Excel 4.0 Macros.</span></span>


### <a name="office-suite"></a><span data-ttu-id="149cb-119">Office 套件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-119">Office Suite</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-120">修正了当来自缓存的 URL 和来自 OneDrive 的 URL 不匹配时，文件将被打开为不同步的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-120">Fixed an issue of file would be opened as NOT SyncBacked when url from cache and url from OneDrive does NOT match.</span></span>



[//]: # (请勿移除错误详细信息内容结尾)

### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="149cb-134">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-134">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-135">我们解决了导致某些会议的原定与会者在其他与会者转发会议时收到取消通知的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-135">We fixed an issue that caused the original attendees of some meetings to receive a cancellation when another attendee forwards the meeting.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-136">我们已修复虽以配置一个或多个签名，但仍导致有的用户在签名下拉菜单中看不到签名的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-136">We fixed an issue that caused some users to see no signatures in the signatures drop down despite having one or more signatures configured.</span></span>

### <a name="office-suite"></a><span data-ttu-id="149cb-139">Office 套件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-139">Office Suite</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-140">Office 套件已修复安装较新版本的 Office 覆盖旧版本时可能因为丢失注册表条目而导致功能受损（例如无法使用 Power Query）的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-140">Office Suite Fixed an issue where installing a newer version of Office over certain older versions can result in impaired functionality (such as being unable to use Power Query) due to missing registry entries.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-167">**使用“高级”对话框创建数据类型：** 在“高级”对话框中，可手动选择合并所创建数据类型的列。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-167">**Use the Advanced Dialog to Create Data Types:** The Advanced Dialog allows you to manually select the columns which combine the Data Type you are creating.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-189">**视频库：** 使用精选和免版税的库提升你的文档应用中提供的免费视频素材</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-189">**Video Library:** Elevate your documents with a library of curated, royalty-free video footage available in-app</span></span>

### <a name="resolved-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="149cb-210">已解决的问题</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-210">Resolved issues</span></span>
### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="149cb-211">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-211">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-212">我们修复了在发送任务状态报告时导致“收件人”字段为空的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-212">We fixed an issue that caused the To field to be blank when sending a status report on a task.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-213">我们修复了导致 MailItem.BeforeAttachmentAdd 事件被破坏的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-213">We fixed an issue that caused the MailItem.BeforeAttachmentAdd event to be broken.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-214">我们添加了一个 regkey，允许客户在 IDataObject 操作中禁用附件的 filetime 包含（例如，拖放、剪贴板）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-214">We added a regkey that allows customers to disable filetime inclusion for attachments in IDataObject operations (i.e. drag drop, clipboard).</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="149cb-215">HKCU\SOFTWARE\Microsoft\Office\16.0\Outlook\Attachments。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-215">HKCU\SOFTWARE\Microsoft\Office\16.0\Outlook\Attachments.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="149cb-216">REG_DWORD IncludeFileTimesInDataObject。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-216">REG_DWORD IncludeFileTimesInDataObject.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="149cb-217">0 = filetimes 被排除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-217">0 = filetimes are excluded.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="149cb-218">1 = （默认）包含 filetime。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-218">1 = (default) filetimes are included.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-219">我们修复了以下问题：当回复带有来自 Azure 信息保护的保护标签的邮件时，将导致嵌入式图像消失。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-219">We fixed an issue that caused inline images to disappear when replying to a message with a protection label from Azure Information Protection.</span></span>


### <a name="powerpoint"></a><span data-ttu-id="149cb-220">PowerPoint</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-220">PowerPoint</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-221">我们修复了 Slide.Shapes.AddMediaObject2 在使用传统的视频格式（MPG-1、Mpeg-2）时会崩溃的 VBA 问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-221">We have fixed a VBA issue where Slide.Shapes.AddMediaObject2 crashing with legacy video formats (MPG-1,Mpeg-2).</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-222">我们修复了以下问题：复制包含新近录制的音频的幻灯片后，保存文件时出现错误。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-222">We fixed an issue where there is an error when saving the file after duplicating a slide that contains a newly recorded audio.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-223">修复了一些损坏的 PowerPoint 文件无法正常打开（即使在执行文档修复操作后也是如此）的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-223">Fixed an issue where some corrupt PowerPoint files were not opening correctly, even after a document repair operation.</span></span>

### <a name="access"></a><span data-ttu-id="149cb-259">Access</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-259">Access</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-260">**跟上时代!日期/时间扩展数据类型具有更好的精度 。:** 引入新的改进的数据类型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-260">**Keep up with the times! The Date/Time Extended data type has better precision.:** Introducing a new and improved data type.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="149cb-261">为了增强与SQL的语法兼容性，并提高包含日期和时间的记录的准确性和详细程度，我们将DateTime2数据类型实现到Access中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-261">To enhance syntax compatibility with SQL, and to increase accuracy and level of detail in records that include dates and times, we’re implementing the DateTime2 data type into Access.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="149cb-262">这个额外的日期和时间数据类型将包括更大的日期范围(0001-01-01通过 9999-12-31)，具有更高的指定时间精度(使用纳秒，而不是秒)，你将能够提供和执行计算。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-262">This additional date & time data type will include a larger date range (0001-01-01 through 9999-12-31), with higher-specified time precision (nanoseconds, rather than seconds) that you will be able to provide and perform calculations on.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="149cb-263">要启用，请选择新字段> Date & Time Extended。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-263">To enable, select New field > Date & Time Extended.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="149cb-264">了解更多</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-264">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/708c32da-a052-4cc2-9850-9851042e0024)

### <a name="teams"></a><span data-ttu-id="149cb-284">Teams</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-284">Teams</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-285">**Microsoft Teams 中的模板：** 使用T eams 中的模板，用户可以在创建新团队时从各种可自定义的模板中进行选择，以帮助他们快速入门。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-285">**Templates in Microsoft Teams:** With Templates in Teams, users can choose from a variety of customizable templates when creating a new team, helping them get started quickly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="149cb-286">IT 专业人员还可以为其组织创建新的自定义模板，从而使他们能够标准化团队结构，展示相关应用程序并扩展最佳实践。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-286">IT professionals can also create new custom templates for their organization, allowing them to standardize team structures, surface relevant apps, and scale best practices.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-287">**固定置顶帖：** 此功能允许用户将频道中的任何消息“固定”到频道信息窗格，以供频道的所有成员查看。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-287">**Pinned Posts:** This feature allows users to "pin" any message in a channel to the channel info pane for all members of the channel to see.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="149cb-288">任何有权访问该频道的成员都将能够看到固定的消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-288">Any members who have access to the channel will be able to see pinned messages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="149cb-289">频道的任何成员都可以固定任何消息（除非通过频道审核设置将其关闭）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-289">Any member of a channel will be able to pin any message (unless turned off via channel moderation settings).</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-290">**提交到应用程序目录：** 您将在此屏幕的左下方看到“提交到应用程序目录”链接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-290">**Submit to app catalog:** You’ll see a Submit to app catalog link on the lower left of this screen.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="149cb-291">除 App Studio 和 Visual Studio 外，还可在此处提交供审批的应用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-291">In addition to App Studio and Visual Studio, it’s another place where you can submit apps for approval.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-292">**在弹出会议体验中将 Freehand by Invision 用于白板：** 现在，可以在参加任何弹出式会议体验的会议中将 Freeman by Invision 应用程序应用至白板。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-292">**Use Freehand by Invision to whiteboard in the popped out meeting experience:** You can now use the Freehand by Invision app to whiteboard in any meeting you take in the popped out meeting experience.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="149cb-293">从共享内容托盘中选择 Freehand 应用程序并进行安装，然后与同事开始白板会话，即可开始集思广益！</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-293">Seamlessly start brainstorming by selecting the Freehand app from the share content tray and, installing it, and starting the whiteboarding session with your colleagues!</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-307">我们修复了导致默认情况下不会为用户打开云设置的 n 问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-307">We fixed a n issue that caused Cloud Settings not to be turned on for users by default.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-308">我们修复了导致用户签名更改无法保存的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-308">We fixed an issue that caused changes to a user's signature to fail to save.</span></span>


### <a name="powerpoint"></a><span data-ttu-id="149cb-309">PowerPoint</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-309">PowerPoint</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-312">修复了以下问题：将项目从 PWA 保存到本地 mpp 文件时，用户实际上未更改的数据将触发 ProjectBeforeTaskChangeEvent。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-312">Fixed an issue where when you save a project from PWA to a local mpp file, the ProjectBeforeTaskChangeEvent fires for data that wasn't actually changed by the user.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-315">修复了以下问题：如果在“任务窗体”类型视图中更改了滞后，ProjectBeforeTaskChange 事件中的 NewVal 没有正确的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-315">Fixed an issue where the NewVal in the ProjectBeforeTaskChange event doesn't have the correct value if a lag is changed within a Task Form type view.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-359">**将形状另存为图片：** 只需单击几下即可将形状、图标或其他对象另存为图片文件，以便您将其用于其他任何位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-359">**Save shapes as pictures:** In just a few clicks, save a shape, icon, or other object as a picture file so you can reuse it elsewhere.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="149cb-360">了解更多</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-360">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/3c4f9ca4-945a-4c33-af91-d10e4e3ea715)

### <a name="teams"></a><span data-ttu-id="149cb-449">Teams</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-449">Teams</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-450">**呼叫合并：**“呼叫合并”使最终用户能够将其现行的未保持 1 对 1 呼叫合并到另一个 1 对 1 呼叫或另一个组呼叫中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-450">**Call Merge:** Call Merge gives end users the capability to merge their active unheld 1-1 call into another 1-1 call or another group call.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="149cb-451">这适用于 Teams VOIP 呼叫和 PSTN 呼叫。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-451">This applies to Teams VOIP calls and PSTN calls.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-452">**管理员可以为其一线工作人员配置基于班次的状态（上班、下班）：** 管理员可以将其一线工作人员配置为具有基于班次的状态：上班、忙碌（上班时可以切换）和下班。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-452">**Admins can configure shift-based presence (On shift, Off shift) for their Firstline workers:** Admins can configure their firstline workers to have shift-based presence states: On shift, Busy (can be toggled when on shift), and Off shift.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-453">**Teams 中的 Cortana 语音技能：** Teams 移动应用中的 Cortana 语音技能可帮助用户仅使用自然语言执行会议、交流和协作任务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-453">**Cortana voice skills in Teams:** Cortana voice skills in Teams mobile app help users perform meeting, communication and collaboration tasks simply using spoken natural language.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="149cb-454">用户可以通过在 Teams 应用中单击麦克风按钮来与 Cortana 对话，如果他们需要在做家务、遛狗或者忙个不停时与他人联系，可以通过该应用来发出“打电话给 Megan”或“给我的下一个会议发消息”等请求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-454">Users can speak to Cortana by clicking on the microphone button in Teams app and make requests like “Call Megan” or “Send a message to my next meeting” if they need to connect with someone while juggling household chores or walking the dog or generally on the go.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="149cb-455">用户只需说“加入我的下一个会议”即可加入会议，或者通过询问“今天早上有哪些工作”来查看日历。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-455">Users can join meetings simply by saying “Join my next meeting” or check their calendar by asking “what do I have this morning”.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="149cb-456">在会议或呼叫中，他们可以在会议阶段从溢出菜单中调用 Cortana，并执行典型的会议中任务，例如按姓名或电话号码添加人员（“将 Megan 添加到呼叫”）、幻灯片组演示（“显示季度回顾幻灯片组”）或浏览幻灯片（“转到附录幻灯片”）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-456">Once in a meeting or a call, they can invoke Cortana from the overflow menu in the meeting stage and perform typical in-meeting tasks like adding people by name or number (“Add Megan to the call”), deck presentation (“present the quarterly review deck”) or navigating slides (“Go to the appendix slide”).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="149cb-457">该功能还支持查找和共享文件、搜索以及在 Teams 应用中进行常规导航（与 John 聊天、转到未读活动、转到我的 @提及等）等事务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-457">Other things that the feature supports are finding and sharing files, search, and generally navigating within the Teams app (“Open my chat with John, Go to my unread activity, Go to my mentions etc.).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="149cb-458">Teams 中的 Cortana 满足[在线服务条款 (OST)](https://www.microsoft.com/licensing/product-licensing/products)中反映的对 Cortana 企业服务的企业级隐私、安全性和合规性承诺。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-458">Cortana in Teams meets the same enterprise-level privacy, security, and compliance promises for Cortana enterprise services, as reflected in the [Online Services Terms (OST)](https://www.microsoft.com/licensing/product-licensing/products).</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-459">**群聊功能增加：** Teams 新增了一项功能，可以进行 250 位参与者的群聊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-459">**Group chat increase:** Teams added the ability to now have 250 participants in a group chat.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-460">**按班次标记：** 通过此功能，将自动为人员分配标记，与他们在 Teams 的 [Shifts 应用](https://support.microsoft.com/office/get-started-in-shifts-5f3e30d8-1821-4904-be26-c3cd25a497d6#bkmk_openshiftsappdesktop)中的日程安排和班次组名称相匹配。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-460">**Tagging by Shift:** With this feature, people are automatically assigned tags that match their schedule and shift group name in the [Shifts app](https://support.microsoft.com/office/get-started-in-shifts-5f3e30d8-1821-4904-be26-c3cd25a497d6#bkmk_openshiftsappdesktop) in Teams.</span></span>

### <a name="word"></a><span data-ttu-id="149cb-461">Word</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-461">Word</span></span>

### <a name="feature-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="149cb-534">功能更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-534">Feature updates</span></span>
### <a name="excel"></a><span data-ttu-id="149cb-535">Excel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-535">Excel</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-536">**建立 PDF 连接：** 连接到 PDF，从其中导入数据，刷新数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-536">**Make a PDF connection:** Connect to, import, refresh data from a PDF.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="149cb-537">了解更多</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-537">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/be4330b3-5356-486c-a168-b68e9e616f5a)

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-538">**不干扰他人筛选和排序：** 现在可以使用工作表视图与他人协作时排序和筛选你的 Excel 文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-538">**Filter and sort without disrupting others:** You can now sort and filter your Excel file while collaborating with others with Sheet View.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="149cb-539">此新增功能可防止你在共同创作文档时受到其他用户的排序和筛选的影响。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-539">This new feature prevents you from being impacted by other user’s sorts and filters while coauthoring the document.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="149cb-540">了解更多</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-540">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/0eea3dc5-d7d1-44c5-a953-25ebfbd6c1a6)

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-541">**自动应用或推荐敏感度标签：** Office 可以根据检测到的敏感内容来推荐或自动应用敏感度标签。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-541">**Auto-apply or recommend sensitivity labels:** Office can recommend or automatically apply a sensitivity label based on the sensitive content detected.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-542">**在 Excel 中从 Power BI 中的数据集创建数据透视表：** 你可以在 Excel 中创建连接到 Power BI 中存储的数据集的数据透视表，只需点击几下鼠标。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-542">**Create PivotTables from Datasets in Power BI within Excel:** You can create PivotTables in Excel that are connected to datasets stored in Power BI with a few clicks.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="149cb-543">这样做可以让你更好地利用数据透视表和 Power BI。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-543">Doing this allows you get the best of both PivotTables and Power BI.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="149cb-544">使用数据透视表从你的安全的 Power BI 数据集计算、总结和分析数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-544">Calculate, summarize, and analyze your data with PivotTables from your secure Power BI datasets.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="149cb-545">了解更多</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-545">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/31444a04-9c38-4dd7-9a45-22848c666884)<br /><span data-ttu-id="149cb-546">在[博客文章](https://blog-insider.office.com/2020/06/11/use-power-bi-data-in-excel/)中查看详细信息</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-546">See details in [blog post](https://blog-insider.office.com/2020/06/11/use-power-bi-data-in-excel/)</span></span>

### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="149cb-547">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-547">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-548">**在 Outlook 中使用快速投票创建投票：** 轻松创建投票、收集选票和在电子邮件中查看结果 [了解详细信息](https://support.office.com/article/46893563-ab12-4bd0-aff7-26f5a488fea0)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-548">**Create polls in Outlook with Quick Poll:** Easily create a poll, collect votes, and view results within an email [Learn more](https://support.office.com/article/46893563-ab12-4bd0-aff7-26f5a488fea0)</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-549">**将图片作为电子邮件一部分发送时，保持图片的高度机密性：** 将图片作为电子邮件内容的一部分发送时，可以使用新的 Outlook 设置限制图片压缩</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-549">**Keep your pictures high fidelity when sending them as part of an email:** A new Outlook setting is available to limit picture compression when you send pictures as part of the email contents</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-550">**快速从上一个 Outlook 会话重新打开项目：** 我们增加了一个选项，使你能快速从上一个 Outlook 会话重新打开项目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-550">**Quickly reopen items from previous session:** We added an option to quickly reopen items from a previous Outlook session.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="149cb-551">无论 Outlook 崩溃或关闭，现在你都可以在重新打开应用时快速重新启动项目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-551">Whether Outlook crashes or you close it, you’ll now be able to quickly relaunch items when you reopen the app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="149cb-552">默认情况下，启用此功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-552">This feature is on by default.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="149cb-553">若要将其关闭，请转到 "选项" > "常规" > "启动选项"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-553">To turn it off, go to Options > General > Start up Options.</span></span>

### <a name="powerpoint"></a><span data-ttu-id="149cb-554">PowerPoint</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-554">PowerPoint</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-555">**自动应用或推荐敏感度标签：** Office 可以根据检测到的敏感内容来推荐或自动应用敏感度标签。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-555">**Auto-apply or recommend sensitivity labels:** Office can recommend or automatically apply a sensitivity label based on the sensitive content detected.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-557">**全新简化通知设置：** 用户现在可以通过增强功能以更简化的方式管理其通知设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-557">**New simplified notification settings:** Users can now manage their notifications settings in a more simplified manner with enhanced functionalities.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-558">**现在 Teams 支持 Windows 本机通知：** 用户现在可以通过团队内置横幅或 Windows 本机横幅选择首选的通知传递方式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-558">**Windows Native Notification are now Supported on Teams:** Users can now select their preferred means of notification delivery, either through teams built in banners or the windows native banners.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-559">**频道信息窗格：** 在频道标题中的“频道信息”图标上进行选择时，将打开一个窗格，可在其中看到频道信息的摘要，包括频道说明、近期参与者和成员列表，以及系统消息的新服务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-559">**Channel Info Pane:** When selecting on the "Channel info" icon in the channel header, a pane will open where you will see a summary of channel information including the channel description, a list of recent contributors and members, as well as the new home for system messages.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-560">**关闭聊天通知预览：** 用户可以更改设置和管理其聊天通知 Toast 的预览。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-560">**Turn off previews for your chat notifications:** Users can change settings and manage previews for their chat notification toasts.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-561">**建议的答复：** 我们为 Teams 用户增加了对他们的对话提出建议答复的功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-561">**Suggested replies:** We added the ability for Teams users to have a suggested reply to their conversations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="149cb-562">如果启用这些建议，它们将显示在聊天消息的底部。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-562">These suggestions will appear at the bottom of a chat message if they are enabled.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="149cb-563">他们使回复消息变得快速而轻松！</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-563">They make replying to messages quick and easy!</span></span>

### <a name="feature-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="149cb-624">功能更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-624">Feature updates</span></span>
### <a name="excel"></a><span data-ttu-id="149cb-625">Excel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-625">Excel</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-626">**更长文件名：** Windows 桌面版 Excel 现在支持名称和路径长达 400 字符的 OneDrive/SharePoint 文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-626">**Longer file names:** Excel for Windows desktop now supports OneDrive/SharePoint files with names and paths of up to 400 characters.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-627">**Realtimedata (RTD) 改进：** 在 Office 365 版本 2002 每月频道或更高版本中，Excel 的 RealTimeData (RTD) 函数要比 Excel 2010 计算电子表格中的数据的速度快得多。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-627">**Realtimedata (RTD) improvements:** In Office 365 version 2002 monthly channel and later, Excel's RealTimeData (RTD) function is much faster than Excel 2010 calculating data in the spreadsheet.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="149cb-628">我们在其基本内存和数据结构中删除瓶颈，并使其变得线程安全，这能允许其在 多线程计算 (MTR) 的所有可用线程上进行计算。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-628">We removed bottlenecks in its underlying memory and data structures as well as made it thread-safe to allow  it to be calculated on all available threads of Multithreaded recalculation (MTR).</span></span>

### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="149cb-629">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-629">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-630">**新增了用于在 Outlook 中撰写邮件时禁用 @提及建议的选项：** 你是否觉得 @提及选取器更令人生厌，而不是更有用？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-630">**New option to disable @ mention suggestions when composing mail in Outlook:** Do you find the @ mention picker more annoying than useful?</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="149cb-631">现在，可以根据需要禁用它。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-631">Now you can turn it off if you prefer.</span></span><br /><span data-ttu-id="149cb-632">在[博客文章](https://blog-insider.office.com/2020/03/26/feedback-in-action-disable-mentions/)中查看详细信息</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-632">See details in [blog post](https://blog-insider.office.com/2020/03/26/feedback-in-action-disable-mentions/)</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-633">**IT 管理员事件通知：** 使用 Outlook for Windows 中的新右侧面板通知，Microsoft 365 租户全局管理员和 Office 应用程序管理员将收到有关影响用户的 Outlook 和 O365 通知。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-633">**Incident Notification for IT Admins:** Microsoft 365 tenant global administrators and Office Apps Administrators will be notified about Outlook and O365 Exchange incidents affecting their users with a new right-side panel notification in Outlook for Windows.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="149cb-634">了解更多</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-634">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/46c07f08-1277-41ce-b353-4e205e9da333)

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-635">**在 Outlook toast 通知中增加了额外的按钮：** 在 Windows 10 上运行 Outlook 时，Outlook toast 通知中会出现快速操作按钮</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-635">**Additional buttons added to Outlook toast notifications:** Quick Action buttons now appear in Outlook toast notifications when running Outlook on Windows 10</span></span>

### <a name="powerpoint"></a><span data-ttu-id="149cb-636">PowerPoint</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-636">PowerPoint</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-637">**改进了 PowerPoint 的流视频性能：** 我们对 Microsoft Stream 视频的回放性能进行了改进，以最小化视频加载时间，创造流畅的观看体验。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-637">**Improved Stream video performance in PowerPoint:** We’ve made improvements to the playback performance of Microsoft Stream videos to minimize video loading time and create a smooth viewing experience.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="149cb-638">使用来自 Microsoft Stream 的企业视频来创建更好的演示文稿。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-638">Use your corporate videos from Microsoft Stream to create better presentations.</span></span>

### <a name="teams"></a><span data-ttu-id="149cb-639">Teams</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-639">Teams</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-640">**外部用户屏蔽了 PSTN 参与者的电话号码：** 对于为 Teams 会议启用了音频会议的客户，我们将向自组织外部加入的用户屏蔽 PSTN 参与者的电话号码。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-640">**PSTN participant phone numbers are masked from external users:** For customers with Audio Conferencing enabled for their Teams meetings, we will mask the PSTN participant's phone number to users who have joined from outside of your organization.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-641">**管理频道通知设置的简化方法：** 通过团队和频道列表或从频道标题中，用户可以通过单击打开或关闭所有活动或深入了解自定义项来设置其首选排列，从而快速管理其通知设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-641">**Simplified way to manage your channel notification settings:** Through the teams and channels list or from the channel header, the users can quickly manage their notification settings by turning all activity on or off with a single click or diving deep into custom to set their preferred permutations.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-642">**Walkie Talkie：** 使用“按下即可发言”进行即时语音通信。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-642">**Walkie Talkie:** Instant voice communication using push-to-talk.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-736">**演示时同步所做的更改：** 即使演示文稿处于幻灯片放映模式，只要进行了更改就同步这些更改。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-736">**Synchronize changes while you are presenting:** Synchronize changes whenever they are made even when the presentation is in slide show mode.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="149cb-737">了解更多详细信息</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-737">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/5a2921a9-97d4-436b-b0cd-295dfe2236bb)<br /><span data-ttu-id="149cb-738">在[博客文章](https://blog-insider.office.com/2020/04/08/synchronize-changes-while-presenting/)中查看详细信息</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-738">See details in [blog post](https://blog-insider.office.com/2020/04/08/synchronize-changes-while-presenting/)</span></span>

Earbuds 设置”下选择“使用手势控制演示”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-742">In Slide Show, right click on the slide and under Surface Earbuds Settings choose Use Gestures to Control Presentation.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="149cb-743">在以后的所有演示中都会记住此设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-743">This setting will be remembered for all future presentations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="149cb-744">现在可以在左侧耳机上向前向后滑动，以在幻灯片放映模式中浏览演示文稿。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-744">You can now can swipe forward and backward on the left earbud to navigate your presentations in Slide Show mode.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="149cb-745">双击播放或暂停嵌入视频。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-745">Double tap to play or pause embedded videos.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="149cb-746">重要提示：必须使用 Windows 10 的 Surface Audio 应用配对 Surface Earbuds，才能使用手势控制演示文稿。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span ### <a name="teams"></a><span data-ttu-id="149cb-749">Teams</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-749">Teams</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-750">**更换为 Teams 会议中的视频版式：** 很快，在 Teams 会议中可以同时查看的与会人员将从 4 人增加到 9 人。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-750">**Changes to video layout in Teams meetings:** Soon, the number of participants that can be viewed simultaneously during a Teams meeting will increase from 4 to 9.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-751">**直播活动中包含音频系统：** 现在，直播活动中的演示者和制作人可以在直播活动中共享桌面或窗口屏幕时包括系统音频。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-751">**Include system audio in live events:** Presenters and producers in live events can now include system audio when sharing a desktop or window screen during the live event.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="149cb-752">这将使您的用户听到所共享内容的任何音频部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-752">This will allow your users to hear any audio part of the content you are sharing.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-753">**使组织者能够更改拨号参与者的会议厅设置：** 此设置控制通过电话拨入的用户是否直接加入会议或在大厅中等待，无需考虑 “自动允许人员” 设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-753">**Enable organizers to change lobby settings for dial-in participants:** This setting controls whether people who dial in by phone join the meeting directly or wait in the lobby regardless of the Automatically admit people setting.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-754">**在会议中举手：** 用户现在可以在会议中举起虚拟手！</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-754">**Raise Your Hand in Meetings:** Users can now raise a virtual hand in a meeting!</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="149cb-755">其他与会者将在会议台的姓名旁或名册的姓名旁看到你举起的手。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-755">Other participants will see your raised hand next to your name in the meeting stage and next to your name in the roster.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-756">**自定义会议视频背景：** 使用视频会议时，现可选择不同的静态背景图像。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-756">**Customize meeting video backgrounds:** When you are meeting with video, you now have the choice of different static background images to use.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="149cb-757">这将让你显示此图像，而不是你所坐位置的实际背景。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-757">This will let you show this image and not the actual background of where you are sitting.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-758">**添加更多人员至聊天：** 现在，我们可以在一个聊天线程中最多添加 350 人。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-758">**Add more people to chat:** We made it possible to now add up to 350 people to a single chat thread.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-759">**活动源“设置”齿轮：** 用户现在可以通过设置齿轮直接从源左栏访问活动源和通知设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-759">**Settings Gear on your Activity Feed:** Users can now directly access activity feed and notification setting from the feed left rail by the means of a settings gear.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-760">**轻松从进行中的 Teams 会议访问选项：** Teams 会议开始后，我们通过直接在参与者窗格中提供易于访问的链接，使会议组织者更快、轻松地更改其演示者和会议厅设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-760">**Easily access meeting options from within a Teams meeting in progress:** We are making it easier for meeting organizers to quickly and easily change their presenter and lobby settings once a Teams meeting starts by providing an easy to access link directly in the participants pane.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="149cb-761">此新功能将同时出现在预定会议和“立即开会”会议中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-761">This new functionality will be present for both scheduled and “Meet Now” meetings.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-762">**团队和频道分析：** 除团队分析之外，现在还可以查看频道级别的指标和见解。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-762">**Team and channel analytics:** In addition to team analytics, now you can also view channel level metrics and insights.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="149cb-763">我们还将时间范围延长到 90 天，因此可以分析更长的数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-763">We've also enhanced the time period to 90 days so you can analyze data for longer periods.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="149cb-764">除此之外，此版本还包括有关团队或渠道的文章、回复和会议数量的新指标和图表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-764">Apart from that, this release also includes new metrics and charts around count of posts, replies and meetings for a team or channel.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-765">**进入/退出公告：** 我们添加了此功能，使会议组织者可以打开或关闭进入和退出会议的公告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-765">**Entry/exit announcements:** We added this feature that lets meeting organizers have the ability to turn on or off entry and exit announcements for a meeting.</span></span>

### <a name="skype"></a><span data-ttu-id="149cb-780">Skype</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-780">Skype</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-781">当用户被告知只能使用团队的策略时，他们仍然可以使用Skype for Business Outlook 插件来安排会议。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-781">When a user is given a policy that moves them to Teams Only, they were still able to use the Skype for Business Outlook add-in to schedule meetings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="149cb-782">在此更新之后，当客户端读取指示用户为仅限团队的策略并进入仅限会议加入模式后，你将不再能够为Skype安排商务会议。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-782">After this update, you will no longer be able to schedule Skype for Business meetings after the client reads the policy indicating the user is Teams Only, and enters meeting join only mode.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="149cb-783">另外，如果 Skype for Business Outlook 插件在启动时看到 Skype for Business客户端处于会议加入模式，它将不会激活自己。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-783">Additionally the Skype for Business Outlook Add-in will not activate itself while starting up if it sees the Skype for Business client is in meeting join only mode.</span></span>

### <a name="office-suite"></a><span data-ttu-id="149cb-784">Office 套件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-784">Office Suite</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-785">此更新修复了 Microsoft Office 中 Visual Basic for Applications 的以下问题：某些引用库名称或库路径中包含 DBSC 字符的代码库的 VBA 项目会被 Office 应用程序视为加载时损坏。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-785">This update fixes an issue in Visual Basic for Applications in Microsoft Office where certain VBA projects that contain references to code libraries with DBCS characters in the library name or library path would be viewed by the Office application as corrupt on load.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-786">此更新修复了 Microsoft Office 中的一个问题，即在运行时可能无法正确找到所含引用可通过搜索 PATH 环境变量中指定的位置找到的 Visual Basic for Applications 项目，从而导致 VBA 运行时错误。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-786">This update fixes an issue in Microsoft Office where Visual Basic for Applications projects with references that are expected to be found by searching locations specified in the PATH environment variable may not be found properly at runtime, leading to VBA runtime errors.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-787">当注册表键HKEY_CURRENT_USER\Software\Microsoft\Internet Explorer\Main\TabProcGrowth被设置为零时，正在激活一个外接程序时，windows中的office主机故障。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-787">The office host was crashing in windows, when an add-in is being activated while the registry key HKEY_CURRENT_USER\Software\Microsoft\Internet Explorer\Main\TabProcGrowth is set to zero.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="149cb-788">此更改可修复此问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-788">This change would fix this issue.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-908">**你喜爱的 Excel 函数运行速度更快：** SUMIFS、AVERAGEIFS、COUNTIFS、MAXIFS 和 MINIFS 函数运行速度比以往更快。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-908">**Your favorite Excel functions just got faster:** The SUMIFS, AVERAGEIFS, COUNTIFS, MAXIFS, and MINIFS functions are much faster than ever before.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="149cb-909">更快达到底线。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-909">Get to the bottom line more quickly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="149cb-910">立即试用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-910">Try one now.</span></span>

### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="149cb-911">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-911">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-912">**将电子邮件拖动到你拥有的组：** 通过从收件箱中拖动来移动和复制邮件和对话。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-912">**Drag email to a group you own:** Move and copy messages and conversations by dragging them from your inbox.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="149cb-913">将与所有组成员共享你拖动的消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-913">Messages you drag will be shared with all group members.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-914">**强制 wifi 网络新体验：** 是否已加入需要使用网页登录的 wifi 网络？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-914">**New experience for captive wifi networks:** Have you ever joined a wifi network that required a web page to sign in with?</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="149cb-915">现在，Outlook 检测到这一点，帮助你进行连接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-915">Outlook now detects this and helps you get connected.</span></span>

###<a name="powerpoint"></a><span data-ttu-id="149cb-916">PowerPoint</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-916">PowerPoint</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-927">在某些情况下，重新打开嵌入 Word 或 PowerPoint 的工作簿时，Excel 会崩溃。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-927">Excel would crash in certain cases when re-opening a workbook embedded in Word or PowerPoint.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-928">解决了如果关闭了源代码簿，则外部链接不会在填充时更新的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-928">Addressed an issue where external links don't update on fill if the source book is closed.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-929">解决了从模板创建图表时出现的性能问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-929">Addressed a performance issue when creating charts from templates.</span></span>

### <a name="onenote"></a><span data-ttu-id="149cb-930">OneNote</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-930">OneNote</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-931">通过暂时将新的嵌入式附件的最大允许大小降低到 50 MB，提升了同步和服务稳定性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-931">Improved sync and service stability by temporarily reducing the maximum allowable size of new embedded attachments to 50MB.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="149cb-932">对于超出此限制的文件，用户可以选择将文件上传到 OneDrive 并将链接插入 OneNote。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-932">For files that exceed this limit, users will have the option of uploading the file to OneDrive and inserting a link into OneNote.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-933">通过临时调整 OneNote 2016 中的同步频率，提升了同步和服务稳定性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-933">Improved sync and service stability by temporarily adjusting sync frequency in OneNote 2016.</span></span>

### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="149cb-934">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-934">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-935">解决了导致用户在退出后在任务管理器中看到 Outlook 进程延迟的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-935">Addressed an issue that caused users to see the Outlook process lingering in task manager after exiting.</span></span>

### <a name="powerpoint"></a><span data-ttu-id="149cb-936">PowerPoint</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-936">PowerPoint</span></span>

### <a name="project"></a><span data-ttu-id="149cb-938">Project</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-938">Project</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-941">解决了以下问题：在标记为完成后，任务完成百分比错误地更改为小于 100% 完成。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-941">Fixed an issue where task percent complete was incorrectly changing to a value less than 100% complete after it was marked complete.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-942">修复了有时无法正确计算摘要任务日期的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-942">Fixed an issue where summary task dates weren't always getting calculated correctly.</span></span>

### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="149cb-1212">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-1212">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-1213">**Outlook 中的插入链接菜单将插入包含租户管理员定义的权限的链接：** Outlook 插入链接 MRU 中的链接将插入仅对已经拥有权限的用户有效的链接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-1213">**Insert Link Menu in Outlook will insert a link with permission defined by tenant admin:** A link from the Insert Link MRU in Outlook would insert a link that only worked for users who already had permissions to it.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="149cb-1214">这通常会导致请求获得文档访问权限的用户之间发生往来电子邮件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-1214">This often caused back and forth emails between users asking to be granted access to a document.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="149cb-1215">我们已更新了此体验，现在该链接将通过租户管理员设置的默认权限进行插入。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-1215">We've updated this experience so now the link is inserted with the default permission set by the tenant admin.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-1216">**Outlook 可视化刷新：** 这是 Outlook 核心体验的可视化刷新的一部分，它更新了邮件在阅读窗格和检查器中的布局方式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-1216">**Outlook visual refresh:** This is part of the visual refresh of core experiences in Outlook, updating how mail messages layout in the reading pane and inspector.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-1217">**共享日历更新速度更快：** 对于 Office 365 中的共享日历，Outlook 可以使用 REST API 更新这些日历。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-1217">**Shared calendar updates just got faster:** For shared calendars in Office 365, Outlook can update these calendars using the REST API.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="149cb-1218">打开预览，更快速、更可靠地更新共享日历。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-1218">Turn on the preview for faster and more reliable updates to shared calendars.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-1219">**查看搜索结果中的相关消息：** Outlook 会分析搜索词，并在搜索结果顶部显示最相关的电子邮件信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-1219">**See relevant messages in your search results:** Outlook analyzes search terms and shows the most relevant email messages at the top of your search results.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="149cb-1220">还会在“热门搜索结果”部分看到按日期排序的所有搜索结果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-1220">You'll also see all results sorted by date in the Top Results section.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-1221">**向合适的人员发送电子邮件：** 只需单击“收件人:”行，然后从建议的联系人中进行选择。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-1221">**Send the mail to the right person:** Just click the To: line and choose from suggested contacts.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="149cb-1222">图片和状态指示器可帮助你选择合适的人员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-1222">A picture and presence indicator helps you choose the right person.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-1223">**针对攻击的高级防护：** 通过 Office 365 高级威胁防护，可通过电子邮件主题中的超链接、附加邮件、签名邮件、网络路径等方式抵御攻击。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-1223">**Advanced protection against attack:** With Office 365 Advanced Threat Protection, you're protected against attacks through hyperlinks within email subjects, attached messages, signed messages, network paths, and so on.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-1224">**以不同的亮度查看邮件：** 使用“太阳”/“月亮”按钮在阅读窗格中的明暗背景之间切换。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-1224">**See your messages in a different light:** Use the Sun/Moon button to switch between light and dark backgrounds in the reading pane.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="149cb-1225">了解更多</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-1225">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/3e2446e0-9a7b-4189-9af9-57fb94d02ae3)

- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-p304">**缩放和粘贴：** 选择默认设置用于所有邮件，而无需在每次阅读邮件时调整缩放。[了解详细信息](https://support.office.com/article/56c090bc-e148-44a7-bd06-1290edd38983)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-p304">**Zoom and stick:** Instead of adjusting Zoom each time you read a message, choose a default to use for all your messages.  [Learn more](https://support.office.com/article/56c090bc-e148-44a7-bd06-1290edd38983)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-1670">**移动邮件时继续工作：** Outlook 现在在后台移动邮件，因此你可以在文件夹之间移动大量邮件时继续工作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-1670">**Keep working while moving messages:** Outlook now moves messages in the background, so you can keep working while moving lots of messages between folders.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-p305">**优化了重点收件箱的启用和禁用体验：** 对于不使用重点收件箱的客户，我们跨所有文件夹恢复了邮件列表中的“未读”选项卡。此外，我们还添加了按标志排序功能，以简化已标志项的查找过程。最后，重点收件箱改进了搜索交互模型：重点收件箱一直保留到用户开始搜索，我们在搜索完成后显示“结果”文本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-p305">**Polished the Focused Inbox on and off experiences:** For customers that do not use Focused Inbox, we brought back the Unread tab in the message list across all folders. We also added a sort by Flag to make it easier to find flagged items. Finally, Focused Inbox has a better interaction model with search: Focused Inbox remains until a user starts to search and we show 'Results' text shown after a search completes.</span></span>

## <a name="version-1807-july-25"></a><span data-ttu-id="149cb-1856">版本 1807：7 月 25 日</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-1856">Version 1807: July 25</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="149cb-1857">*版本 1807（内部版本 10325.20082）*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-1857">*Version 1807 (Build 10325.20082)*</span></span>

### <a name="outlook-feature-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="149cb-1858">Outlook：功能更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-1858">Outlook: Feature updates</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-p339">**Outlook 加载项警告：** Outlook COM 加载项有时会遇到导致 Outlook 其余部分运行速度变慢的问题。这些问题可能是由事件延迟导致的，例如在 Outlook 文件夹之间切换、新邮件的到达、正在打开日历项目等。出现此类问题时，Outlook 将在通知栏中显示一条警告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-p339">**Outlook add-in warnings:** Occasionally an Outlook COM add-in can encounter problems that slows down the rest of Outlook. These problems could be due to latency of events such as switching between Outlook folders, arrival of new emails, opening Calendar items, etc. When such issues arise, Outlook will display a warning in the notification bar.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="149cb-p340">**从“Outlook 提醒”对话框加入团队会议：** 当 Outlook 提醒用户参加即将召开的会议时，如果即将召开的会议是团队在线会议，则它将显示一个“联机加入”按钮。这与从“Outlook 提醒”对话框加入 Skype for Business 会议的体验类似。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-p340">**Join Teams meetings from the Outlook Reminders dialog:** When Outlook reminds users of an upcoming meeting, it will show a Join Online button if the upcoming meeting is a Teams online meeting. This is similar to the experience of joining a Skype for Business meeting from the Outlook Reminders dialog.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="149cb-2107">修复了在没有音频的情况下配置 Skype for Business 以加入会议时，添加音频到会议会对用户本人启动一个新的 P2P 呼叫，而不是添加音频到现有会议的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-2107">Fix an issue where, when Skype for Business is configured to join meetings without audio, adding audio to a meeting initiates a new P2P call to the user itself rather than adding audio to the existing meeting.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="149cb-2108">修复了以下问题：在 Outlook 中单击会议请求内的“加入 Skype 会议”链接时，用户看到“找不到此 Skype 会议”错误消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="149cb-2108">Fix an issue where user receives the error message "We couldn't find this Skype meeting" when clicking 'Join Skype Meeting' link in a meeting request from Outlook.</span></span>
